aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_R_i6mjbiinpfiulb_" data-state="closed" class="operation-target inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 p-1.5 no-underline 11.9452C13.3328 12.7274 12.7277 13.352 11.967 13.6899L11.4286 13.9292C11.1202 14.0662 11.1202 14.5144 11.4286 14.6515L11.9989 14.9049C12.7406 15.2344 13.3349 15.8367 13.6649 16.5932L13.85 17.0174C13.9855 17.328 14.4155 17.328 14.5511 17.0174ZM13.7809 14.2852L14.2028 13.8662L14.6159 14.2852L14.2028 14.6924L13.7809 14.2852Z" fill="#525252"></path></svg>Open in<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down text-tertiary" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This endpoint returns a pre-signed URL that you can use to download a PDF document related to the specified <a href="/docs/healthcare/transaction-enrollment">transaction enrollment</a>.</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Call this endpoint with the document ID for the PDF document you want to download. The document ID is returned in the responses for the <a href="/docs/healthcare/api-reference/get-enrollment">Retrieve Enrollment</a> and <a href="/docs/healthcare/api-reference/get-enrollment-list-enrollments">List Enrollments</a> endpoints.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The endpoint returns a pre-signed URL that you can use to download the specified PDF document.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Use a <code>GET</code> request to download the PDF document from the pre-signed URL.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="code-block not-prose group relative my-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border text-sm outline-none !bg-black h-auto [--shiki-light:#D4D4D4] [--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4] shiki shiki-themes stedi-custom stedi-custom" style="--shiki-light:#D4D4D4;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4;--shiki-light-bg:#0A0A0A;--shiki-dark-bg:#0A0A0A" tabindex="0"><button aria-label="Copy Text" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 bg-transparent hover:bg-transparent hover:text-gray-100 cursor-pointer absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] text-quaternary" type="button"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon absolute transition-transform"><path d="M6.9998 6V3C6.9998 2.44772 7.44752 2 7.9998 2H19.9998C20.5521 2 20.9998 2.44772 20.9998 3V17C20.9998 17.5523 20.5521 18 19.9998 18H16.9998V20.9991C16.9998 21.5519 16.5499 22 15.993 22H4.00666C3.45059 22 3 21.5554 3 20.9991L3.0026 7.00087C3.0027 6.44811 3.45264 6 4.00942 6H6.9998ZM5.00242 8L5.00019 20H14.9998V8H5.00242ZM8.9998 6H16.9998V16H18.9998V4H8.9998V6Z"></path></svg></button><div class="text-[13px] py-3.5 overflow-auto [&amp;_.line]:px-4 fd-scroll-container h-full"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CA8A04;--shiki-dark:#CA8A04">curl</span><span style="--shiki-light:#3B82F6;--shiki-dark:#3B82F6"> --request</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CA8A04;--shiki-dark:#CA8A04"> GET</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D7BA7D;--shiki-dark:#D7BA7D"> \</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D4D4D4;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">--url </span><span style="--shiki-light:#CA8A04;--shiki-dark:#CA8A04">&quot;&lt;downloadUrl&gt;&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D7BA7D;--shiki-dark:#D7BA7D"> \</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D4D4D4;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">--output </span><span style="--shiki-light:#CA8A04;--shiki-dark:#CA8A04">/path/to/file.pdf</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
</li>
</ol>
<p>You can also download enrollment documents manually from the enrollment&#x27;s details page in the Stedi portal.</p><div class="flex items-end justify-between gap-2"><h2 class="flex scroll-m-28
